LAW DEPARTMENT
LIST OF NOTARIES APPOINTED AND PRACTICE AT THE BEGINNING OF THE YEAR 2009.
(See Rule 17)
[G.O. Ms. No.11, Law (Administration) Department, 30th January 2009.]
No. II(2)/LAW/51(c)/2009.

the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby publishes the following list of Notaries appointed by the Government
of Tamil Nadu and in practice at the beginning of the year 2009 :—
